         <h3>
          Our Services
         </h3>
        </div>

     </div>
     <div class="container">
      <div class="row isotope" id="isotope-service-container">
       <div class=" col-md-4 service">

         <div class="enigma_service_iocn pull-left">
          <i class="fa-language">
          </i>
         </div>
         <div class="enigma_service_detail media-body">
          <h3>
           <a href="">
            Language services
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
          </p>
          <div class="skype-share" data-href="http://www.esentranslation.com/" data-lang="auto" data-source="WordPress" data-style="large">
          </div>
          <div style="clear:both;padding-bottom:10px;">
          </div>
          <p class="MsoNormal">
           ESEN Translation Services is pleased to offer its clients various language services. These include: translation, interpretation (phone or in-person), proofreading, editing, transcription and language instruction (individual and group, online).
          </p>
          <p>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class=" col-md-4 service">
        <div class="enigma_service_area appear-animation bounceIn appear-animation-visible">
         <div class="enigma_service_iocn pull-left">
          <i class="fa-plane">
          </i>
         </div>
         <div class="enigma_service_detail media-body">
          <h3>
           <a href="#">
            Wanna Go Where?
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
          </p>
          <div class="skype-share" data-href="http://www.esentranslation.com/" data-lang="auto" data-source="WordPress" data-style="large">
          </div>
          <div style="clear:both;padding-bottom:10px;">
          </div>
          <p>
           Have you ever wanted to move abroad? Take a peek at “Wanna Go Where”?, a short guide to the ins and outs of moving abroad. If you’re still at the “I wonder if…” stage as regards a decision, then this guide is for you. You can find it on sale at Amazon, Barnes &amp; Noble, and other online bookstores.
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class=" col-md-4 service">
        <div class="enigma_service_area appear-animation bounceIn appear-animation-visible">
         <div class="enigma_service_iocn pull-left">
          <i class="fa-university">
          </i>
         </div>
         <div class="enigma_service_detail media-body">
          <h3>
           <a href="#">
            Crash Courses
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
          </p>
          <div class="skype-share" data-href="http://www.esentranslation.com/" data-lang="auto" data-source="WordPress" data-style="large">
          </div>
          <div style="clear:both;padding-bottom:10px;">
          </div>
          <p>
           We also offer language crash courses for those who need a lot of specific instruction â for instance, for Spanish language tests at your company, or a month-long trip to your company’s Latin American office â in a short period of time. And, if you already know Spanish or Quichua, but want to reduce your non-native accent, we’ll be glad to help!
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
